Subject: [Carpediem] Communicating Science at Wellesley this Saturday
Message-ID: <DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE4013598548FDE@EXVS01.olin.edu>

Tl;dr: Communicating Science Symposium at Wellesley this Saturday, 10:30am-=
2:30pm at the Pendleton Atrium. Breakfast and lunch are served. You should =
go.
Here's the link to the website where you can register<https://sites.google.=
com/site/wellesleycommsci/>. (free)
Here's a google spreadsheet where you can organize rides<https://docs.googl=
e.com/spreadsheet/ccc?key=3D0AoUHHbVj5DaCdENaeW1xaFZReHN1bFB2MnVXTFhkOWc&us=
p=3Dsharing> (but you could bike too, depending on the weather)


Here's some more detailed information!

Concept Note, "Communicating Science 2014: Environmental Health and Biotech=
nology"


We live in a society where science is central to policy decisions around co=
mplex issues and is therefore often politicized. For example, policy discus=
sion around climate change mirrors a large disconnect between scientific co=
nsensus and public perception; while there is a 97% consensus among climate=
 scientists that anthropogenic climate change is a reality, only 47% of Ame=
ricans believe in the science. There are also a sharp partisan divide over =
the issue, which is influenced by political and economic stakeholders who w=
ant the science on their side. While climate change is a well-known example=
 of the need for more effective science communication, there are many other=
 important issues where this is the case: genetic modification, the effects=
 of prenatal drugs, and environmental toxins. This has profound effects on =
the well-being and sustainability of our society and environment.


To understand the depth of the problem our society faces in communicating s=
cience and to discuss potential solutions for systemic change, the annual W=
ellesley Communicating Science Symposium brings together scientists, journa=
lists, and activists for a day of dialogue and problem-solving. Since 2010,=
 our Communicating Science symposia have brought together several hundred p=
eople from Wellesley, surrounding universities, and the Boston community to=
 discuss the complexities around communicating science to policy makers and=
 the public. Previous keynote speakers have included Elizabeth Grossman, Ja=
mes Hansen, and Matthew Nisbet. Panelists have included Environmental Healt=
h Services journalist Wendy Hessler, Wellesley College President Kim Bottom=
ly, and many others.

The 2014 Communicating Science Symposium seeks to address issues relating t=
o communicating environmental health and biotechnology research to the publ=
ic and policy makers. Terms like "genetically modified organism" have becom=
e taboo, as many people associate these modern technologies as harmful to t=
he environment and risks to human health. The symposium will address challe=
nges to communicating the science behind these complex issues to the public=
 and policy makers. Professor Rita Colwell, a renowned environmental microb=
iologist at the University of Maryland at College Park, former president of=
 the American Association for the Advancement of Science, and long-time dir=
ector of the National Science Foundation, will be our keynote on the subjec=
t. Following her address, a panel featuring speakers from the biotech indus=
try, journalists, and environmental health advocates will further the dialo=
gue on communicating the science of biotechnology. An afternoon networking =
session showcasing student research from schools in the Boston area will ex=
tend the day's conversation to practical applications, giving students agen=
cy and direction in their own scientific pursuits. The symposium will provi=
de a useful forum for the pursuit of solutions to communicating science and=
 the education of students and the general public.

Dear Carpe,
I'm running an informal study in the next 5 weeks to test the effect of a b=
rain training technology called the NeuroTracker  (link<http://neurotracker=
.net/#/training/4554099917>) on participants' standardized test scores.

Participants will take two 15-minute segments of a GMAT, and then will eith=
er train with the NeuroTracker for 5 x 30 minutes or be assigned to a contr=
ol group before writing another version of the tests at the end of the seme=
ster. You're eligible unless you are prone to getting headaches from lookin=
g at 3D screens for ~30 minutes. The GMAT testing will take place in a team=
  room. The Neurotracker training will take place in my dorm room (EH220). =
There will be snacks!

Please reply to this email if you are interested!
Graham

2:30pm at the Pendleton Atrium. Breakfast and lunch are served. You should =
go.
Here's the link to the website where you can register<https://sites.google.=
com/site/wellesleycommsci/>. (free)
Here's a google spreadsheet where you can organize rides<https://docs.googl=
e.com/spreadsheet/ccc?key=3D0AoUHHbVj5DaCdENaeW1xaFZReHN1bFB2MnVXTFhkOWc&us=
p=3Dsharing> (but you could bike too, depending on the weather)

From William.Saulnier at students.olin.edu  Tue Mar  4 10:28:02 2014
From: William.Saulnier at students.olin.edu (William Saulnier)
Date: Tue, 4 Mar 2014 10:28:02 -0500
Subject: [Carpediem] Potential Public Speaking OSS/IS - Planning + Survey
Message-ID: <DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE4013596C9FAA3@EXVS01.olin.edu>

Hi friends,

I'm in the process of designing an OSS on Public Speaking. It would potentially be a full 4/2 credit OSS/IS for a full grade and everything! However, I want to hear what people have to say about Public Speaking (of course!) so the course can be structured in the way that most benefits Oliners.

The joke is everyone fears public speaking, even more than death. And when asked why they fear public speaking more, they answer, "Well, when I'm dead I don't have to give a speech."

Everyone's been in that situation of paralysis, where the words just won't come out the right way, or you're up all night practicing your flash cards and then you stumble over them as you stand up in front of the panel, shifting back and forth. Or maybe you're in a job interview, and the interviewer asks you a question that throws you off guard. Or perhaps you're at your best friends wedding, and he's asked you to write a toast and you don't know where to start. Maybe you're speaking is littered with ums, ya knows, and so ons, and what nots, and you want to eliminate them before you go up in front of an audience at the conference. This OSS would be a chance for you to practice, practice, practice, and enter any situation, from formal events to casual interviews, from presentations to improv, with the skills and confidence to say you don't fear public speaking, you welcome it.

Here's a short survey you can fill out to help me get a good idea for what people might wants

https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1gR9yR9XQk7t-wK_78RYUWVhSgqq6YBW8Qop9uuR4rXQ/viewform

Answer as much as you feel comfortable!

If you have any comments, concerns, questions, demands, or outrage that Charley Nolan already does a Co-Curricular on it so why do we need an OSS, please email me and I'll get back to you!

Yours,

William Saulnier

Hi Carpe/ Helpme!
I am offering you a free ride to Eliot (or the grocery store or train station or anywhere else in Needham/ Wellesley/ Newton) at any time of your choosing in the future!  In fact, I will even both drop you off and pick you up at Eliot! Wow! 

How do you earn this free ride to Eliot? The corollary is that we need to be dropped off (leaving around 8:30 pm) so that you have access to my car to pick us up.  Either leg of the journey earns you a free ride at any point of your choosing in the future-- so one trip -> one free ride; both drop-off and pick-up ->two free rides.  Alternatively, we can just pay you.

Thanks everyone!
Chloe and Annie

Subject: [Carpediem] Internship Opportunity at the Executive Office of the
	President
Message-ID: <DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE4013596C9FAAB@EXVS01.olin.edu>

Hello friends.

Still need work this summer? Want to work with the government on coding projects? I worked for the Software Automation Technology Team at the White House last summer, and it was a blast! First years, this is a great chance to have a wonderful experience, pick up some technical skills that will help for future opportunities, and meet the people that make the government work. If you're interested, shoot me an email or check out the listing on USA Jobs. It's something that I enjoyed greatly and I bet you will too.

         https://www.usajobs.gov/GetJob/ViewDetails/362720700
 
As always, you can get to the application from the SWAT page at:
 
                http://www.whitehouse.gov/SWATIntern

Hope this helps in your search for Internships!

Yours,

-William Saulnier

Gaby

ml

nts on the mountain.

so if you're interested let me know!

An Olin alum's friend is looking for a technical cofounder in a startup.
Information and contact info below!

-Jordyn

---
Sloan & MIT Media Lab student looking for technical co-founder for fitness =
hardware startup
Karma is an interactive yoga mat hardware startup that tracks, analyzes and=
 provides real-time feedback on how to improve your form, maximize your bal=
ance, and redefine your yoga fitness regimen. With the explosive success of=
 fitness tracking devices today, this high tech mat would push hardware to =
the next level by providing a highly personalized, self-correcting fitness =
experience based on the user's movements and stats. The mat and app would a=
llow users to accurately do poses that build strength, flexibility, and bal=
ance.
The yoga industry has experienced robust annual growth of 7.7%. Currently, =
22 million adults practice yoga and accessories spend is over $10.2 billion=
. Companies have also built successful empires around yoga, including Lulul=
emon (IPO in 2007) and Zico (acquired by Coke in 2013).
As an advanced yogi with 12 years of experience, I have witnessed firsthand=
 the growth in yoga demographics and the recent crossover of yoga into spor=
ts training (check out Marathon Man<http://www.cnn.com/2012/09/04/health/ru=
nners-need-yoga/index.html?hpt=3Dhp_c2> and NFL<http://online.wsj.com/news/=
articles/SB10001424052702303496804579369043641774378>).  Yoga has the far-r=
eaching market potential to encompass all sports, either as the focal point=
 or ancillary form of training. I have spent the past 3 months researching =
market validation and establishing relationships with fitness studios. Prio=
r to MIT, I spent 5 years covering the consumer and health industries in fi=
nance and sales. Now, I am looking for a co-founder to both lead and build =
the technology side of the business.
If you're interested in the intersection of fitness and technology, the cha=
llenge of creating and designing a new product, and leading the tech vision=
 for Karma, please get in touch with me at patchen at mit.edu<mailto:patchen at m=
it.edu>.
[cid:CC437B07-6A35-4925-9AB9-1A907A451D32]

TLDR: Olin students can join the Wellesley Sailing Team, meeting tonight @ =
Wellesley, 7pm in the Lulu campus center 416

If you didn't know, Olin students can race with the Wellesley Sailing team.=
 I've been competing with the team for 4 years and came in knowing nothing =
about sailing. There is a meeting tonight at Wellesley if you'd like to joi=
n the team.

It's an amazing opportunity, and beginners are welcome! We have a coach, we=
 teach newer teammates to sail, we practice racing on the charles river out=
 of the MIT Boathouse, and compete in intercollegiate sailing regattas with=
 teams from all over.

I'm driving over at around 6:30pm tonight. Feel free to give me a call or a=
n email with your number if you'd like a ride.
-Chris Mark

g spring break. Normal Olin hourly rate applies.

Let me know if you're interested.

Thanks,

Did you watch the Toy Story movie and feel like Sid, the kid who creatively=
 remixed his toys, should have been the star and not the bad guy? [Yes, his=
 toys were a bit creepy http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hXCxVIUUBPw/T1kfFrhLVHI/A=
AAAAAAAAGg/yz23gi4qSbU/s1600/sidstoys.jpg but creative nonetheless.]

If you want to satisfy your inner-Sid, take a look at  Autodesk=92s Franken=
Tech challenge - weekly invitations to use the new Fusion 360 design tool t=
o fuse together two unsuspecting technologies into a monster model (I.e., w=
hat do you get when a camcorder and a Beats-by-Dre speaker hook up at a par=
ty and have a baby?). Weekly winners get their wacky ideas sent to them in =
a 3D-printed model=85 but more importantly get bragging rights over other s=
tudents FrankenTinkering with my butt-based CAD tool (who are probably pr=
ocrastinating under the pressure of too many pre-spring break deadlines).

Information is here: https://frankentech.autodesk.ballistiq.com/ and (https=
://www.facebook.com/Autodeskedcommunity).

Take care,
Amon

-sorry if I stir up old nightmares with the imagery above. This email is ra=
ted PG-13. No pieces of technology were harmed in its creation.

From William.Saulnier at students.olin.edu  Thu Mar 13 19:45:59 2014
From: William.Saulnier at students.olin.edu (William Saulnier)
Date: Thu, 13 Mar 2014 19:45:59 -0400
Subject: [Carpediem] Dominos Pizza Order: Coder's Edition
Message-ID: <DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE40136D0379010@EXVS01.olin.edu>

tl;dr Domino's order going out at 8:30ish. 9 dollars nets you anything off the 599 menu, with special requests accepted on a case by case basis. Will accept payment via venmo or cash in person.

for student in olinCollege:
  hunger = student.checkHunger()
  if hunger && Time.now() <= Time("8:30PM"):
    student.want("bread with toppings")
    student.checkWebpage(http://dominos.com)
    order = student.decide()
    student.email(olinColege.findStudentByName("William Saulnier"), order)
    student.venmoUser("lego6245 at gmail.com", 9)
    student.waitForEmail()

Hi Everyone!

I wanted to follow up on our "interesting conversation" a couple of weeks a=

n and specifically around the potential to bring a dedicated computing spac=
e to Olin. I have put together a rough draft of a proposal.  I tried to avo=
id getting too detailed with regards to implementation, instead focusing on=
 motivating the case for the facility and outlining the requirements that m=
ust be met to fully realize the vision.

If people have a bit of time over break, I could really use input to help i=
mprove / flesh out this document.  Additionally, there are some parts where=
 I explicitly ask for student input (particularly testimonials / specific a=
necdotes around why this facility would bring a new dimension to Olin).

The link below will allow you all to view the document but not edit it.  If=
 you would like to edit the document, please request that I give you edit p=
ermissions via the Google Docs interface.  Also, please feel free to share =
this with anyone that doesn=92t get this e-mail and is interested in this i=
nitiative.

https://docs.google.com/document/d/1-b035wc3EQUG07ER-vbZlmK-3fnNCxkhKLf9s17=

ooterLeftAccent.png]

Our Mission:
Making masterworks meaningful through performances
that excite, engage, and inspire,
and through outreach efforts across all ages.
Founded in 1940, Masterworks Chorale is one of the leading choruses in the =
Boston area and an active part of the region's musical community.  Led by c=
onductor Steven Karidoyanes, Masterworks draws its committed singers, profe=
ssional orchestra and talented soloists from throughout New England. The Ch=
orale performs a three-concert series at Sanders Theatre, Cambridge, offers=
 popular community Sings at the holidays and in the summer, and provides in=
tergenerational outreach opportunities.

[https://imgssl.constantcontact.com/letters/images/1101116784221/PM_B2CEP_F=
ooterRightAccent.png]

Hello all!

Hannah Wilk and I are doing a Passionate Pursuit in voice acting this semes=
ter, and are currently producing Much Ado About Nothing in an audiobook, wh=
ich will eventually be put up on Project Gutenberg. We're looking for a few=
 more guys to voice some parts. The time commitment will probably be about =
4 hours on one weekend, and we'll have pizza and drinks while we record.

Email me and Hannah if you're interested, and with a character name if you =
have a particular one in mind. You can find the cast of characters, and the=
 play, here: http://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/2240

Thanks!

Raagini

Subject: [Carpediem] Seeking participants for a brain-training research study
Message-ID: <DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE40136D0FF4AAF@EXVS01.olin.edu>

--_000_DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE40136D0FF4AAFEXVS01oline_
Content-Type: text/plain; charset="us-ascii"
Content-Transfer-Encoding: quoted-printable

Hello,
I'm running an informal study in the next 5 weeks to test the effect of a b=
rain training technology called the NeuroTracker  (link<http://neurotracker=
.net/#/training/4554099917>) on participants' standardized test scores.

Participants will take two 15-minute segments of a GMAT, and then will eith=
er train with the NeuroTracker for 5 x 30 minutes or be assigned to a contr=
ol group before writing another version of the tests at the end of the seme=
ster. You're eligible unless you are prone to getting headaches from lookin=
g at 3D screens for ~30 minutes. The GMAT testing will take place in a team=
  room. The Neurotracker training will take place in my dorm room (EH220). =
There will be snacks!

Please reply to this email if you are interested!
Graham

---------- Forwarded message ----------
From: "CJ Carr" <emperorcj at gmail.com<mailto:emperorcj at gmail.com>>
Date: Mar 19, 2014 11:17 PM
Subject: [burners] Berklee Music Therapy Hackathon 3/28 3pm @ hack/reduce
To: "burners boston" <burners at bostonburners.org<mailto:burners at bostonburners.org>>
Cc:

Hey Burners! This is right down your ally.

Berklee College and hack/reduce are hosting an all-night hackathon for
music therapy! We need programmers and engineers to build tools to empower
everyone to engage the creative spirit of music, regardless of ability or
disability! $5000 grand prize!

Watch promo <http://www.berklee.edu/music-therapy/hack-videos>
*RSVP here*:
http://www.berklee.edu/music-therapy/music-therapy-hackathon-registration


What?

Music therapists help people access music, regardless of their abilities or
disabilities, and use music to help them communicate, express themselves,
and enhance their lives. This first-of-a-kind event will create a space for
hackers to develop innovative tools for music therapists to use in
therapeutic and healthcare settings. This Berklee Music Therapy
Hack--cohosted by Berklee College of Music and hack/reduce--aims to create
a new vision of what music therapy does and can do.
How?

Practicing music therapists and music therapy students will present hack
participants with problems to be solved in real-life settings. Assisted by
a group of expert mentors, teams will have 24 hours to prototype innovative
ideas using state-of-the-art technology and tools. Teams will then present
their projects to a distinguished panel of judges, who will ultimately
award a $5,000 cash prize for the best hack.
When?

3pm Friday, March 28, 2014 till
8pm Saturday, March 29, 2014

*Even if you don't hack, come for presentations @ 6pm Saturday*
Where?

hack/reduce
275 3rd Street
Cambridge, MA 02142
What should I build?

Curious about the needs of music therapy? Check out the project wish
list<http://www.berklee.edu/music-therapy/berklee-music-therapy-hack-teams>
made
by Berklee's music therapy students!




? CJ Carr (organizer)
[cortexel.us<http://cortexel.us>] <http://cortexel.us/> [github] <http://github.com/cortexelus>

burners at bostonburners.org<mailto:burners at bostonburners.org>

Hey Peoples!

It's finally that time. You went on spring break, and saw a bunch of really=
 sexy looking people.

Sadly you were not one of them.

While everyone else was going for their New Year Resolutions at the gym, yo=
u were partying it up with some pizza bagels on the couch.
You were afraid of all the scary, intimidatingly beautiful people on the be=
aches of _______. But, you also kind of want to be like them....

WELL HERE IS YOUR CHANCE!

Fit Club is hosting its first ever super extreme post-spring break transfor=
mation competition (or FESEPSBTC for short, obviously).

All you have to do to participate is go to...
P:\+Clubs_and_StudentGroups\Fit Club\Spring 2014\Before
and upload a photo of you from the front and one of you from the side by MA=
RCH 29TH.
These photos can be in normal clothes, tight fitting clothes, swimsuit, or =
whatever you want... just don't be naked.
Note: The transformation is probably more visible when you are not wearing =
a shirt.
(There is a text document for file naming guidelines. If you wish to remain=
 anonymous, please write a random name and block your face from your photo.=
 Then email me with your secret identity so the prize can be awarded.)



Then, right before finals (and binge eating and depression munchies), we wi=
ll upload our "after" photos.

Winners, decided by an elite panel of non-experienced and completely unknow=
ledgeable of judges, will receive the inaugural FESEPSBTC bro tanks as well=
 as a tub of protein powder of their choosing.


Also join the Fit Club mailing list here:
https://lists.olin.edu/mailman/listinfo/fitclub


Please respond with any questions, comments or concerns, and happy lifting!



--_000_DA80C3E6C10BE94E8FCACEB239C2FEE40136D0FF4C72EXVS01oline_

[cid:image002.jpg at 01CF46BC.3C2557F0]TL;DR:  Come hiking between finals and =
expo when you don't have any work.

NTL;R:
Outing club will be organizing a hiking trip to Mt. Monadnock in southern N=
H for the Saturday between finals and expo (May 10, 2014).  Monadnock is a =
great little mountain, not too strenuous, but a very interesting hike.  Vie=
ws from the top are amazing.

Tentative plan is leave Olin around 7am Saturday morning, get to Monadnock =
around 9am, and start hiking.  It's possible that this will even be free, i=
f not, it should come out to less than $10 per person, to cover gas & the p=
ark entrance fee.

Signup is here<https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1TN7a8Z3Znf298n_tudw7lrZgs1v=
jHwwJ9JSaDR5tbSA/edit>, put yourself down if you think there's any chance y=
ou want to go.

I sent out this signup way early so that we could see how many people might=
 want to go, to see what the SAC funding situation might be.  If you put yo=
ur name down, I'll get in touch with you closer to the date of the actual h=
ike with more details.

Also, for interested parties, I'd love to do some weekend hikes to some of =
the closer by rec areas around here as the weather gets better:  Blue Hills=
 is about 20 minutes away, Leominster State Forest is about an hour away.  =
Email me if you'd also be interested in doing some hikes in April, and hope=
fully we can organize something.

Hey there folks!

The Robotics Lab introduces RobotX - a new robot-related extracurricular at=
 Olin.  Olin college, with MIT, is representing the USA in Singapore this c=
oming fall with our large, motorized, autonomous pontoon boat - and we need=
 your help!

This is a great opportunity for anyone interested in sensors, autonomy, dat=
a handling, vehicle control, boats, travel, competition, etc and so forth!

If you're interested, contact myself, Victoria Coleman, or Dave Barrett for=
 more details.  We would love to have you!

Thanks,
V

w.robotx.org/

It's time for the Needham Spelling Bee again. Held annually, the Bee presen=
ts the opportunity for Olin to field up to two 3-person teams for this fun =
community event. If you're a good speller and would like to represent Olin,=
 please contact me, Joe Hunter, at joseph.hunter at olin.edu<mailto:joseph.hun=
ter at olin.edu> and let me know of your interest. I will follow up with more =
details. In the case that we have more than six people interested, the sele=
ction will be based on the order I receive the responses. The Bee will be h=
eld April 9 beginning at 7 pm in the Needham High gym.

Joe Hunter

You know those people who are called one name but have a different email? I=
sn't that confusing? Those people are the worst.

Like Brooks Willis! He's the worst. His email is christopher.willis at student=
s.olin.edu<mailto:christopher.willis at students.olin.edu>. How confusing.

Solution!

1.      Make a new email, and type the person's email into one of the field=
s

[cid:image001.jpg at 01CF49A1.49B84890]

2.      Right-click on the person's email, and select 'Add to Outlook Conta=
cts'

3.      Change the 'Display as:' field to the name that makes sense to you

a.      Note: you can also change them to a nickname or something else amus=
ing

At this point your can just type in their 'Display as' name and Outlook wil=
l auto-correct.
[cid:image003.jpg at 01CF49A7.113B2A90]

People whose names you might want to correct
I've changed these people so far in my Outlook, I'm sure there are others. =
Just to get you started. Some of these (Jimmy, Ben) you might have no troub=
le remembering. Also, some of these people already have aliases, but unless=
 you already know that it doesn't help you.

-          Henry Horsey              -> Ry Horsey

-          Hongda Yi                    -> Louis Yi

-          Ji Hyung Hong             -> Suzie Hong

-          Christopher Willis       -> Brooks Willis

-          Qun Zeng                    -> Annie Zeng

-          Rebecca Rifkin                        -> Nicole Rifkin

-          James Wu                    -> Jimmy Wu

-          Chu-Hao Fan               -> Jack Fan

-          Franz Schneider          -> Eric Schneider

-          A Young (Claire) Keum           -> Claire Keum

-          Bernard Kahle             -> Ben Kahle

-          Abraham Levitan        -> Abe Levitan

-          Junjie Zhu                    -> Jason Zhu

-          William Warner                      -> Bill Warner

-          Yuxin Guan                  -> Janice Guan

-          Yevgeniya Zastavker   -> Zhenya Zastavker

-          Michael Crowell-Ingram-> Mac-I Crowell-Ingram

-          Forrest Bourke                        -> Forrest 'Ace' Bourke

Other suggestions: Primary Morse/Ruthven, Chris Lee (STUDENT) and Chris Lee=
 (TEACHER), Shanuel Skikne, Greg 'What a butt' Edelston, etc.

et paid) I can ask if that's alright as well.  Let me know if you're intere=

Suzanne
